< text>
This is a great facility in San Macros, conveniently located   in the middle of the san Diego county, in which help for all the teams to come and play  tournaments.

Parking is little tight here but they do have multiple entry points to the park, so you can plan accordingly. I would suggest to look at the Google map to see the various entry points so that you can street park and get into the park conveniently.

This park have 7 baseball fields and 3 patches for throw practices.  They do how multiple restaurant areas and booth for snacks and coffee.

If you have smaller kids there is a play area right in the center of the park and it's convenient for the families to drop that kids and watch the game.

The perk for parents, there are multiple micro breweries around this park so feel free to have a beer or 2 after the game.<//text>

Lindsay and her team are amazing!!! When we decided to sell our home and move across the country, we learned that we would need to not only pack a large house with a lot of stuff, but we needed to pack most of it well before our move so that the house would be attractive to potential buyers. When looking at my busy schedule, I got really stressed out and could not figure out a time that my wife and I would accomplish this between our jobs and taking care of our 5 year old.

I spoke with Lindsay and she (and the team) came to our house a few days before the first showings of the house. They told us exactly how to prepare for them and they packed up nearly 80% of our belongings making our home look spectacular. They had all of our packed stuff in easy to read labeled boxes, so if we need to access certain things that were packed, we were able to do so.

The team then returned 2 days before the movers arrived to pack our remaining belongings and they got it all done in one day.

They move quickly and efficiently while not compromising the integrity of the packing job. We had initially bought moving boxes from another company of which we ended up returning almost all of them. A Smart Move uses the best boxes and packing material which made me feel very confident to my stuff would be safe.

Aside from the great packing job they did, they not only gave me piece of mind during a very stressful period in life, but they also helped facilitate so many other aspects of my move. She found us a cross-country moving company that saved us thousands of dollars as well as a company to transport our 2 cars. Not only did she find these companies for us, but she also worked as a liaison for us and ensured everything went smoothly with them!

I am so happy with their services and would recommend them to any person making a move, local or long-distance.</review>

I have used A Smart Move for 2 moves now and can't recommend them enough. Moving is hard enough without worrying about how many cardboard boxes to get in what sizes, buying packing tape, buying more boxes because cardboard can't carry too much weight, running out of packing tape, not being able to stack boxes very high, boxes being tough to carry, then breaking down all of the cardboard and trying to get rid of it (definitely won't all fit in your recycle bin, does anyone you know need boxes?).

A Smart Move eliminates all of these problems. They make it easy to figure out how many boxes you need. Pricing is easy to find and completely transparent. Reserving is super simple; you pick the delivery and pickup dates and times, add on any extras you need, then simply wait for the boxes to arrive. The "boxes" are heavy duty plastic crates that can handle a ton of weight, are all one size, stack easily whether empty or full, and come with special dollies that make moving the stacks around a breeze. The boxes come with labels and don't require tape, so the only things you'll need are markers and bubble wrap!

<Rating>5</Rating><Review>Found myself around the corner from Slick Fork and gave it a try. Ordered a chicken plate, tri-tip sandwich, pulled pork sandwiches, side of corn bread, coleslaw and mac n cheese. SlickFork did not disappoint! The crew at the window was chill, and the easy going kind of fun professionalism that befits a BBQ joint. Clean tables, modern feel, EXCELLENT FLAVOR. I can't say that enough...... EXCELLENT FLAVOR.

I ordered takeaway and salivated for the 20 minute drive home as the various aromas filled my car. 20 minutes of imagination  can really kill a meal if you're taking all the smells in and the reality doesn't live up to the a vivid imagination.  But this..... oh.. the meat just melted  on the tongue. Perfect flavor blend, just enough sweet, just enough spice and neatly balanced against the raw onion and pickle on the pulled pork. By far the best pulled pork I've had on the west coast. Corn bread was the right size portion, filling without the dryness. The slaw was a nice punch of crisp color and texture to complete my meal. Just that good.

As for the tri-tip, chicken and mac n cheese... all I heard was chewing and intermittent sighs of pleasure between bites. A good sign from an otherwise chatty crew.

In all, definitely 5 stars. The kind of place you make sure to bring out of town family and friends  to. I'm pretty sure their menu is available online. Be sure to come and order early in the day before they sell out... this is a meal you don't want to miss!<//Review><pics>None<//pics>< response>
